<p><b>бо́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жий</b>

***бой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a> (672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bojь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰoyh₂ós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰeyh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike, hew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with typical Indo-European nominal <i>o</i>-ablaut.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бои́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>боёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beating, breakage</li>
<li>battle, combat, engagement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукопашный.html>рукопа́шный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rukopášnyj <b>boj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hand-to-hand <b>fight(ing)/combat</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fight, fighting, struggle</li>
<li>striking <i>(of a clock)</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 3; -moz-column-count: 3; -ms-column-count: 3; -o-column-count: 3; -webkit-column-count: 3;">
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баталия.html>бата́лия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">batálija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boy</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boy <i>(servant)</i>
<ul><li><span style="color:777777">(The addition of quotations indicative of this usage is being sought):</span></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bojьkъ</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bójkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бойче́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бойче́й</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бо́йче</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бойкий.html>бо́йкий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smart, clever</li>
<li>sharp</li>
<li>glib, fluent</li>
<li>animated, busy, brisk</li></ol>

***бойня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бойня.html>бо́йня</a> (14668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойня.html>бо́йня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bójnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойня.html>бо́йни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойня.html>бо́йни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бойня.html>бо́ен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>massacre <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">intentional mass killing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>abattoir <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">public slaughterhouse</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">boccale</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bokál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass, goblet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молоды́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпить.html>вы́пили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бокал.html>бока́лу</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переодеться.html>переоде́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Molodýje výpili po <b>bokálu</b>, pereodélisʹ i pojéxali na vokzál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The young ones drank by the glass, changed clothes and headed off to the train station. —Tolstoy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъlvanъ</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolván</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blockhead, dimwit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">stupid person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>по́нял</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:требоваться.html>тре́бовалось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>bolván</b> tak i ne pónjal štó ot nevó trébovalosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This idiot couldn't understand what was required from him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dummy (in card games)</li>
<li>block <i>(for hats or wigs)</i></li></ol>

***болванка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нка</a> (24927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болван.html>болва́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolván</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolvánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болванка.html>болва́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pig, ingot, blank, block of wood, etc., serving as raw material for some product.</li>
<li>hat block, wig block, blockhead</li>
<li><i>(artillery)</i> solid projectile <i>(either armor-piercing or used as a proof shot)</i>; penetrator round; shot</li>
<li>draft outline, outline</li>
<li><i>(wiki slang)</i> stub</li>
<li><i>(office slang)</i> template, boilerplate</li>
<li>stupid woman, dummy.</li>
<li><i>(computer slang)</i> a blank CD-R /DVD-R / DVD+R <i>etc.</i> disk, or other blank optical media for burning data onto it</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезненный.html>болезненно</a> (7950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненный.html>боле́зненный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boléznennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненный.html>боле́зненно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boléznenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>painfully <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a painful manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненный.html>боле́зненный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boléznennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненность.html>боле́зненность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boléznennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненность.html>боле́зненности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненность.html>боле́зненности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезненность.html>боле́зненностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sickliness, unhealthiness</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнетворный.html>болезнетво́рный</a> (31271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boléznʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:творить.html>твори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pathogenes</i>. First attested in 1786.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнетворный.html>болезнетво́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boleznetvórnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>malignant; causing disease</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнетворный.html>болезнетво́рный</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-знь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-znʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boléznʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́зней</a></b>)

***болеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a> (1467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be sick, to be ill, to be ailing
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворать.html>хвора́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xvorátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be anxious, to be apprehensive</li>
<li>to cheer, to root for
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> спарта́к.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>boléjet</b> za Sparták.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He cheers for Spartak.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt, to ache
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> golová.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a headache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my head.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуб</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> zub.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a toothache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my tooth.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боли́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolít</b> górlo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a sore throat.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my throat.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боля́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolját</b> glazá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My eyes hurt.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my eyes.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боля́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>bolját</b> nógi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My legs ache.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">There is pain in my legs.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***болото.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a> (2510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boloto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swamp; mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бла́то</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bláto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">bláto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swamp; mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">błoto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolóto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болото.html>боло́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bog, swamp, marsh, quagmire, mire</li></ol>

***болтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a> (3042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьltati</i>. Cognate with Polish bełtać ("to stir")
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boltátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dangle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подоконник.html>подоко́ннике</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:джинсы.html>джи́нсах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенно.html>соверше́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомый.html>незнако́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядька.html>дя́дька</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na podokónnike sidél i <b>boltál</b> nogámi v džínsax soveršénno neznakómyj djádʹka.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On the window sill sat an a complete stranger, in jeans, <b>dangling</b> his feet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shake, to rock, to stir</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stir, to mix, to beat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:литый.html>ли́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перестать.html>переста́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложка.html>ло́жкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:похлебка.html>похлёбку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Líta na mgnovénije dáže perestála <b>boltátʹ</b> lóžkoj poxljóbku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Lita in an instant even stopped <b>beating</b> her soup with a spoon.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to babble, to talk needlessly or endlessly</li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бола.html>бол</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>та́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-болт-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>Болта́ть</a> + <i>твор. п</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзоваться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a> (прич. страд. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́емый</a></i>).
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядочный.html>беспоря́дочно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевелить.html>шевели́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:перемещать.html>перемеща́ть</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болтаться.html>болта́ться</a> (4558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтаться.html>болта́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boltátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dangle, to hang about</li>
<li>to loaf, to lounge about</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
